                                            <script type='text/javascript'>
function readCookie(name) {
    var nameEQ = name + "=";
    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for ( var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0) == ' ')
            c = c.substring(1, c.length);
        if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0)
            return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
    }
    return null;
}

var pl_did = readCookie("pl_did");
var pl_p = localStorage.pl;

                                                        <div class="pr dsense "><div class="cid" id="cald4-1-3"></div> <h3 class="dsense_h"><span class="hw dsense_hw">clear</span> <span class="pos dsense_pos" title="A word that describes a noun or pronoun.">adjective</span> <span class="guideword dsense_gw" title="Guide word: helps you find the right meaning when a word has more than one meaning">
            (<span>NOT MARKED OR CLOUDY</span>)

                        <div class="pr dsense "><div class="cid" id="cald4-1-9"></div> <h3 class="dsense_h"><span class="hw dsense_hw">clear</span> <span class="pos dsense_pos" title="A word that describes a noun or pronoun.">adjective</span> <span class="guideword dsense_gw" title="Guide word: helps you find the right meaning when a word has more than one meaning">
            (<span>NOT TOUCHING</span>)
      </span></h3> <div class="sense-body dsense_b"><div class="def-block ddef_block " data-wl-senseid="ID_00005763_13">
                        <div class="dwl hax">
	        <a amp-access="loggedIn" amp-access-hide class="dwla wordlist-add-button" title="Add this meaning to a word list" on="tap:AMP.setState({ stateGlobal: { wlSenseId: 'ID_00005763_13' } }), sidebarWordList.open">

                <div class="ddef_h"><span class="def-info ddef-info">  </span><div class="def ddef_d db">not <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/touching" title="touching">touching</a> something, or away from something: </div> </div><div class="def-body ddef_b"><div class="examp dexamp"><span class="eg deg">Only one <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/competition" title="competitor">competitor</a> made a clear <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/jump" title="jump">jump</a> of the <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/high" title="highest">highest</a> <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/fence" title="fence">fence</a> <span class="gloss dgloss">(= <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/jump" title="jumped">jumped</a> over it without <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/touching" title="touching">touching</a> it)</span>.</span></div><div class="examp dexamp"> <span class="eg deg">When we're clear <span class="b db">of</span> the <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/main" title="main">main</a> <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/road" title="road">road</a>, we'll <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/stop" title="stop">stop</a> for <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/our" title="our">our</a> <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/picnic" title="picnic">picnic</a>.</span></div> </div></div></div>

                <div class="ddef_h"><span class="def-info ddef-info">  <span class="gram dgram"><a href="/help/codes.html">[ <span class="gc dgc">I</span> or <span class="gc dgc">T</span> ]</a></span></span> <div class="def ddef_d db">to (<a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/cause" title="cause">cause</a> a <span class="nondv-xref dnondv-xref"><a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/cheque" title="cheque">cheque</a></span> to) go from one <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/bank" title="bank">bank</a> to another through a <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/central" title="central">central</a> <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/organization" title="organization">organization</a>, so that <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/money" title="money">money</a> can be <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/paid" title="paid">paid</a> to the <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/person" title="person">person</a> it is <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/owe" title="owed">owed</a> to: </div> </div><div class="def-body ddef_b"><div class="examp dexamp"><span class="eg deg">It usually <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/take" title="takes">takes</a> four to five <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/working" title="working">working</a> <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/day" title="days">days</a> for a <a class="query" href="https://dictionary.cambridge.org/dictionary/english/cheque" title="cheque">cheque</a> to clear.</span></div> </div></div></div>
